NOTICE ...

NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICES
P. Selvaraj, a male child born to S. Ponnusamy on 20th January 1989 residing at No. 74, Kayalpatinam Road,
Tiruchendur-628 215, Thoothukkudi District., has been living as a female after an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery
by Dr. Thep Vechavisit, M.D., Pratunam Polyclinic, Bangkok-10400, Thailand. This has been proved after a detailed study
of my medical history, by Dr. Jayaraman MS, former Professor and Head Department of Burns, Plastic & Reconstructive
surgery, Kilpauk Medical College Hospital, Chennai-10. By this, I, may be treated as a female and shall hence forth be
known as P. SHANAVI.
Thoothukkudi,
17th April 2014.

P. SELVARAJ.

TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE

1163

G. Sinthan was born as a male child to (late) L. Ganapathy on 18th June 1987 residing at Railway quarters No. 8C,
North Colony Ezhil Nagar, Dindigul-624 005. After an Elaborate Sexual Reassignment Surgery, she has been living as a
Female (Reference Dr. Ramaling Birge Patil, Shivam Viswa Multi Speciality Hospitals, Bangalore-43. and Dr. Theresa
Valarmathi, ADMO/HU/DG. Southern Railway). The Plant Surgery shows that I could be treated as a Female G. SINTHAN
shall be known as G. SINDHU.
Dindigul,
17th April 2014.

G. SINTHAN.

K. Sathish Kumar a male child born to A. Kandhasamy on 10th June 1991 residing at No. 36, Ghandhi Road,
Kottaimedu, Mallasamuthiram Post, Thiruchengode Taluk, Namakkal-637 503, has been living as female after an elaborate
Sexual Reassignment Surgery by native method which has been confirmed by Dr. K. Mahadevan, M.D.D.V., Professor of
STD, Coimbatore Medical College & Hospital, Coimbatore-18. By this I may treated as a Female and shall henceforth be
known as K. SANTHIYA.
Namakkal,
17th April 2014.

K. SATHISH KUMAR.

I, C. Senthilkumar, Biological son of Thiru RM. Chinnasamy, residing at No. 10, Kali Amman Koil Street, Pallathur,
Karaikudi-630 107, by way of this public notice I inform that (late) Thiru S.P. Ramasamy has legally adopted me as his son
on 26th August 1983 by way of registered deed bearing No. 32/1983 on the Sub-Registrar Office Karaikudi-630 001,
My adopted father (late) Thiru. SP. Ramasamy passed away on (9th February 1992). Here after I shall be
known as a RM. SENTHILKUMAR.
Karaikudi,
17th April 2014.

C. SENTHILKUMAR,
